301→\tmeta[\"showSettings\"] = meta[\"canEdit\"]\n   302→\n   303→\teditable, _ := dashboard[\"editable\"].(bool)\n   304→\tif meta[\"canSave\"] == true && !editable {\n   305→\t\tmeta[\"canMakeEditable\"] = true\n   306→\t} else {\n   307→\t\tmeta[\"canMakeEditable\"] = false\n   308→\t}\n   309→\n   310→\tmeta[\"hasUnsavedFolderChange\"] = false\n   311→\n   312→\t// If dashboard is not editable, restrict permissions\n   313→\tif !editable {\n   314→\t\tmeta[\"canEdit\"] = false\n   315→\t\tmeta[\"canDelete\"] = false\n   316→\t\tmeta[\"canSave\"] = false\n   317→\t}\n   318→}\n   319→\n   320→// removeNullValuesFromVariables removes null values from variable.current.value\n   321→func removeNullValuesFromVariables(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n   322→\ttemplating, ok := dashboard[\"templating\"].(map[string]interface{})\n   323→\tif !ok {\n   324→\t\treturn\n   325→\t}\n   326→\n   327→\tlist, ok := templating[\"list\"].([]interface{})\n   328→\tif !ok || len(list) == 0 {\n   329→\t\treturn\n   330→\t}\n   331→\n   332→\tfor _, item := range list {\n   333→\t\tif variable, ok := item.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   334→\t\t\tif current, ok := variable[\"current\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   335→\t\t\t\tif value, exists := current[\"value\"]; exists {\n   336→\t\t\t\t\t// Check for null value\n   337→\t\t\t\t\tif value == nil {\n   338→\t\t\t\t\t\tdelete(current, \"value\")\n   339→\t\t\t\t\t} else if valueArray, isArray := value.([]interface{}); isArray {\n   340→\t\t\t\t\t\t// Check for null values in arrays\n   341→\t\t\t\t\t\thasNull := false\n   342→\t\t\t\t\t\tfor _, v := range valueArray {\n   343→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif v == nil {\n   344→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\thasNull = true\n   345→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n   346→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   347→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   348→\t\t\t\t\t\tif hasNull {\n   349→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdelete(current, \"value\")\n   350→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   351→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   352→\t\t\t\t}\n   353→\t\t\t}\n   354→\t\t}\n   355→\t}\n   356→}\n   357→\n   358→// ensureQueryIds ensures all queries have refId\n   359→func ensureQueryIds(panel map[string]interface{}) {\n   360→\ttargets, ok := panel[\"targets\"].([]interface{})\n   361→\tif !ok || len(targets) == 0 {\n   362→\t\treturn\n   363→\t}\n   364→\n   365→\t// Check if any target is missing refId\n   366→\thasMissingRefId := false\n   367→\tfor _, target := range targets {\n   368→\t\tif targetMap, ok := target.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   369→\t\t\tif targetMap[\"refId\"] == nil {\n   370→\t\t\t\thasMissingRefId = true\n   371→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   372→\t\t\t}\n   373→\t\t}\n   374→\t}\n   375→\n   376→\tif hasMissingRefId {\n   377→\t\t// Find existing refIds\n   378→\t\texistingRefIds := make(map[string]bool)\n   379→\t\tfor _, target := range targets {\n   380→\t\t\tif targetMap, ok := target.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   381→\t\t\t\tif refId, ok := targetMap[\"refId\"].(string); ok {\n   382→\t\t\t\t\texistingRefIds[refId] = true\n   383→\t\t\t\t}\n   384→\t\t\t}\n   385→\t\t}\n   386→\n   387→\t\t// Assign refIds to targets that don't have them\n   388→\t\tletters := \"ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ\"\n   389→\t\tletterIndex := 0\n   390→\n   391→\t\tfor _, target := range targets {\n   392→\t\t\tif targetMap, ok := target.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   393→\t\t\t\tif targetMap[\"refId\"] == nil {\n   394→\t\t\t\t\t// Find next available refId\n   395→\t\t\t\t\tfor letterIndex < len(letters) {\n   396→\t\t\t\t\t\trefId := string(letters[letterIndex])\n   397→\t\t\t\t\t\tif !existingRefIds[refId] {\n   398→\t\t\t\t\t\t\ttargetMap[\"refId\"] = refId\n   399→\t\t\t\t\t\t\texistingRefIds[refId] = true\n   400→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n   401→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   402→\t\t\t\t\t\tletterIndex++\n   403→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   404→\t\t\t\t\tletterIndex++\n   405→\t\t\t\t}\n   406→\t\t\t}\n   407→\t\t}\n   408→\t}\n   409→}\n   410→\n   411→// getPanels extracts all panels from the dashboard (including nested panels)\n   412→// This matches the frontend's depth-first iteration order in panelIterator()\n   413→func getPanels(dashboard map[string]interface{}) []map[string]interface{} {\n   414→\tvar panels []map[string]interface{}\n   415→\n   416→\t// Get top-level panels\n   417→\tif dashboardPanels, 420→\t\t\t\t// Add top-level panel first\n   421→\t\t\t\tpanels = append(panels, panel)\n   422→\n   423→\t\t\t\t// Then add its nested panels (depth-first order)\n   424→\t\t\t\tif nestedPanels, ok := panel[\"panels\"].([]interface{}); ok {\n   425→\t\t\t\t\tfor _, nestedPanelInterface := range nestedPanels {\n   426→\t\t\t\t\t\tif nestedPanel, ok := nestedPanelInterface.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   427→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tpanels = append(panels, nestedPanel)\n   428→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   429→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   430→\t\t\t\t}\n   431→\t\t\t}\n   432→\t\t}\n   433→\t}\n   434→\n   435→\treturn panels\n   436→}\n   437→\n   438→// cleanupPanelForSaveWithContext mimics the PanelModel.getSaveModel() behavior\n   439→// This removes properties that shouldn't be persisted and filters out default values\n   440→func cleanupPanelForSaveWithContext(panel map[string]interface{}, isNested bool) {\n   441→\t// Apply auto-migration logic (matches frontend PanelModel constructor)\n   442→\t// This happens during cleanup phase to match when frontend applies auto-migration\n   443→\t// Only apply auto-migration to top-level panels, not nested ones (matches frontend behavior)\n   444→\tif !isNested {\n   445→\t\tapplyPanelAutoMigration(panel)\n   446→\t}\n   447→\n   448→\t// Library panel specific cleanup (matches frontend behavior)\n   449→\t// Frontend only preserves id, title, gridPos, and libraryPanel for library panels\n   450→\tif libraryPanel, hasLibraryPanel := panel[\"libraryPanel\"]; hasLibraryPanel && libraryPanel != nil {\n   451→\t\t// Create a new panel with only the essential properties\n   452→\t\tessentialProps := map[string]interface{}{\n   453→\t\t\t\"id\":           panel[\"id\"],\n   454→\t\t\t\"title\":        panel[\"title\"],\n   455→\t\t\t\"gridPos\":      panel[\"gridPos\"],\n   456→\t\t\t\"libraryPanel\": libraryPanel,\n   457→\t\t}\n   458→\n   459→\t\t// Clear the original panel and copy back only essential properties\n   460→\t\tfor key := range panel {\n   461→\t\t\tdelete(panel, key)\n   462→\t\t}\n   463→\t\tfor key, value := range essentialProps {\n   464→\t\t\tif value != nil {\n   465→\t\t\t\tpanel[key] = value\n   466→\t\t\t}\n   467→\t\t}\n   468→\t\treturn // Skip the rest of the cleanup for library panels\n   469→\t}\n   470→\n   471→\t// Row panel specific cleanup (matches frontend behavior)\n   472→\tcleanupRowPanelProperties(panel)\n   473→\n   474→\t// Track which properties were present in the input to preserve them even if they become empty\n   475→\toriginalProperties := make(map[string]bool)\n   476→\tfor key := range panel {\n   477→\t\toriginalProperties[key] = true\n   478→\t}\n   479→\t// Properties that should never be persisted (notPersistedProperties)\n   480→\tnotPersistedProps := map[string]bool{\n   481→\t\t\"events\":                  true,\n   482→\t\t\"isViewing\":               true,\n   483→\t\t\"isEditing\":               true,\n   484→\t\t\"isInView\":                true,\n   485→\t\t\"hasRefreshed\":            true,\n   486→\t\t\"cachedPluginOptions\":     true, // This is the key one causing issues\n   487→\t\t\"plugin\":                  true,\n   488→\t\t\"queryRunner\":             true,\n   489→\t\t\"replaceVariables\":        true,\n   490→\t\t\"configRev\":               true,\n   491→\t\t\"hasSavedPanelEditChange\": true,\n   492→\t\t\"getDisplayTitle\":         true,\n   493→\t\t\"dataSupport\":             true,\n   494→\t\t\"key\":                     true,\n   495→\t\t\"isNew\":                   true,\n   496→\t\t\"refreshWhenInView\":       true,\n   497→\t\t\"scopedVars\":              true, // Frontend removes scopedVars from save model\n   498→\t}\n   499→\n   500→\t// Default values that should be filtered out if they match (defaults)\n   501→\tdefaults := map[string]interface{}{\n   502→\t\t\"gridPos\": map[string]interface{}{\n   503→\t\t\t\"x\": float64(0), \"y\": float64(0), \"h\": float64(3), \"w\": float64(6),\n   504→\t\t},\n   505→\t\t\"targets\": []interface{}{\n   506→\t\t\tmap[string]interface{}{\"refId\": \"A\"},\n   507→\t\t},\n   508→\t\t\"cachedPluginOptions\": map[string]interface{}{},\n   509→\t\t\"transparent\":         false,\n   510→\t\t\"options\":             map[string]interface{}{},\n   511→\t\t\"links\":               []interface{}{},\n   512→\t\t\"fieldConfig\": map[string]interface{}{\n   513→\t\t\t\"defaults\":  map[string]interface{}{},\n   514→\t\t\t\"overrides\": []interface{}{},\n   515→\t\t},\n   516→\t\t\"title\": \"\",\n   517→\t}\n   518→\n   519→\t// Remove notPersistedProperties\n   520→\tfor prop := range notPersistedProps {\n   521→\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n   522→\t}\n   523→\n   524→\t// Filter out properties that match defaults\n   525→\tfor prop, defaultValue := range defaults {\n   526→\t\tif panelValue, exists := panel[prop]; exists {\n   527→\t\t\tif isEqual(panelValue, defaultValue) {\n   528→\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n   529→\t\t\t}\n   530→\t\t}\n   531→\t}\n   532→\n   533→\t// Remove empty transformations array unless nested panel had them originally\n   534→\tif transformations, ok := panel[\"transformations\"].([]interface{}); ok && len(transformations) == 0 {\n   535→\t\tif panel[\"_originallyHadTransformations\"] != true || !isNested {\n   536→\t\t\tdelete(panel, \"transformations\")\n   537→\t\t}\n   538→\t}\n   539→\n   540→\t// Remove null values recursively to match frontend's JSON.stringify/parse behavior\n   541→\t// Pass panel type information to help with threshold handling\n   542→\tpanelType := \"\"\n   543→\tif t, ok := panel[\"type\"].(string); ok {\n   544→\t\tpanelType = t\n   545→\t}\n   546→\tremoveNullValuesRecursivelyWithContext(panel, panelType)\n   547→\n   548→\t// Filter out properties that match defaults (matches frontend's isEqual logic)\n   549→\tfilterDefaultValues(panel, originalProperties)\n   550→\n   551→\t// Clean up internal markers\n   552→\tdelete(panel, \"_originallyHadTransformations\")\n   553→\tdelete(panel, \"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\")\n   554→}\n   555→\n   556→// filterDefaultValues removes properties that match the default values (matches frontend's isEqual logic)\n   557→func filterDefaultValues(panel map[string]interface{}, originalProperties map[string]bool) {\n   558→\t// Get panel type for panel-specific defaults\n   559→\tpanelType := \"\"\n   560→\tif t, ok := panel[\"type\"].(string); ok {\n   561→\t\tpanelType = t\n   562→\t}\n   563→\n   564→\t// PanelModel defaults from frontend\n   565→\tdefaults := map[string]interface{}{\n   566→\t\t\"gridPos\": map[string]interface{}{\n   567→\t\t\t\"x\": 0, \"y\": 0, \"h\": 3, \"w\": 6,\n   568→\t\t},\n   569→\t\t\"targets\": []interface{}{\n   570→\t\t\tmap[string]interface{}{\"refId\": \"A\"},\n   571→\t\t},\n   572→\t\t\"cachedPluginOptions\": map[string]interface{}{},\n   573→\t\t\"transparent\":         false,\n   574→\t\t\"options\":             map[string]interface{}{},\n   575→\t\t\"links\":               []interface{}{},\n   576→\t\t\"fieldConfig\": map[string]interface{}{\n   577→\t\t\t\"defaults\":  map[string]interface{}{},\n   578→\t\t\t\"overrides\": []interface{}{},\n   579→\t\t},\n   580→\t\t\"title\": \"\",\n   581→\t}\n   582→\n   583→\t// Add panel-specific defaults\n   584→\tif panelType == \"table\" {\n   585→\t\t// Remove legacy table properties (matches frontend getSaveModel filtering)\n   586→\t\t// Exception: preserve original properties for old table panels with autoMigrateFrom=\"table-old\"\n   587→\t\tlegacyTableProps := []string{\"pageSize\", \"scroll\", \"fontSize\", \"showHeader\", \"sort\"}\n   588→\t\tfor _, prop := range legacyTableProps {\n   589→\t\t\tif _, exists := panel[prop]; exists {\n   590→\t\t\t\tif autoMigrateFrom, hasAutoMigrate := panel[\"autoMigrateFrom\"]; hasAutoMigrate && autoMigrateFrom == \"table-old\" {\n   591→\t\t\t\t\tif !originalProperties[prop] {\n   592→\t\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n   593→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   594→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   595→\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n   596→\t\t\t\t}\n   597→\t\t\t}\n   598→\t\t}\n   599→\t}\n   600→\n   601→\t// Remove properties that match defaults, but preserve properties that were originally present\n   602→\tfor prop, defaultValue := range defaults {\n   603→\t\tif panelValue, exists := panel[prop]; exists {\n   604→\t\t\tif isEqual(panelValue, defaultValue) {\n   605→\t\t\t\t// Special case: fieldConfig - handle preservation of original custom object first\n   606→\t\t\t\tif prop == \"fieldConfig\" {\n   607→\t\t\t\t\t// Check if we need to preserve the custom object before removing fieldConfig\n   608→\t\t\t\t\tif panel[\"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\"] == true {\n   609→\t\t\t\t\t\t// Ensure fieldConfig structure exists with custom object\n   610→\t\t\t\t\t\tif fieldConfig, ok := panelValue.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   611→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif defaults, ok := fieldConfig[\"defaults\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   612→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif _, hasCustom := defaults[\"custom\"]; !hasCustom {\n   613→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdefaults[\"custom\"] = map[string]interface{}{}\n   614→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   615→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t// Don't remove fieldConfig if we added custom back\n   616→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   617→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   618→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   619→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   620→\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n   621→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   622→\t\t\t\t\t// Only remove if it wasn't originally present in the input\n   623→\t\t\t\t\tif !originalProperties[prop] {\n   624→\t\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n   625→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   626→\t\t\t\t}\n   627→\t\t\t}\n   628→\t\t}\n   629→\t}\n   630→\n   631→\t// Remove empty targets arrays (frontend removes them in cleanup)\n   632→\tremoveIfDefaultValue(panel, \"targets\", []interface{}{})\n   633→\n   634→\t// Handle case where fieldConfig was removed but originally had custom object\n   635→\tif panel[\"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\"] == true {\n   636→\t\tif _, hasFieldConfig := panel[\"fieldConfig\"]; !hasFieldConfig {\n   637→\t\t\t// Recreate fieldConfig with custom object\n   638→\t\t\tpanel[\"fieldConfig\"] = map[string]interface{}{\n   639→\t\t\t\t\"defaults\": map[string]interface{}{\n   640→\t\t\t\t\t\"custom\": map[string]interface{}{},\n   641→\t\t\t\t},\n   642→\t\t\t\t\"overrides\": []interface{}{},\n   643→\t\t\t}\n   644→\t\t}\n   645→\t}\n   646→\n   647→\t// Clean up fieldConfig to match frontend behavior\n   648→\tif fieldConfig, exists := panel[\"fieldConfig\"].(map[string]interface{}); exists {\n   649→\t\t// Clean up fieldConfig defaults to match frontend behavior\n   650→\t\tif defaults, hasDefaults := fieldConfig[\"defaults\"].(map[string]interface{}); hasDefaults {\n   651→\t\t\t// Remove properties that frontend considers as defaults and omits\n   652→\t\t\tcleanupFieldConfigDefaults(defaults, panel)\n   653→\n   654→\t\t\t// Preserve custom object if it was originally present, even if empty\n   655→\t\t\tif panel[\"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\"] == true {\n   656→\t\t\t\tif _, hasCustom := defaults[\"custom\"]; !hasCustom {\n   657→\t\t\t\t\tdefaults[\"custom\"] = map[string]interface{}{}\n   658→\t\t\t\t}\n   659→\t\t\t}\n   660→\t\t}\n   661→\t}\n   662→}\n   663→\n   664→// isEqual checks if two values are equal (simplified version)\n   665→func isEqual(a, b interface{}) bool {\n   666→\tif a == nil && b == nil {\n   667→\t\treturn true\n   668→\t}\n   669→\tif a == nil || b == nil {\n   670→\t\treturn false\n   671→\t}\n   672→\n   673→\t// For simple types, use direct comparison\n   674→\tswitch aVal := a.(type) {\n   675→\tcase bool:\n   676→\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(bool); ok {\n   677→\t\t\treturn aVal == bVal\n   678→\t\t}\n   679→\tcase string:\n   680→\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(string); ok {\n   681→\t\t\treturn aVal == bVal\n   682→\t\t}\n   683→\tcase float64:\n   684→\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(float64); ok {\n   685→\t\t\treturn aVal == bVal\n   686→\t\t}\n   687→\tcase []interface{}:\n   688→\t\tif bVal, ok := b.([]interface{}); ok {\n   689→\t\t\tif len(aVal) != len(bVal) {\n   690→\t\t\t\treturn false\n   691→\t\t\t}\n   692→\t\t\tfor i, v := range aVal {\n   693→\t\t\t\tif !isEqual(v, bVal[i]) {\n   694→\t\t\t\t\treturn false\n   695→\t\t\t\t}\n   696→\t\t\t}\n   697→\t\t\treturn true\n   698→\t\t}\n   699→\tcase map[string]interface{}:\n   700→\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   701→\t\t\tif len(aVal) != len(bVal) {\n   702→\t\t\t\treturn false\n   703→\t\t\t}\n   704→\t\t\tfor k, v := range aVal {\n   705→\t\t\t\tif !isEqual(v, bVal[k]) {\n   706→\t\t\t\t\treturn false\n   707→\t\t\t\t}\n   708→\t\t\t}\n   709→\t\t\treturn true\n   710→\t\t}\n   711→\t}\n   712→\n   713→\treturn false\n   714→}\n   715→\n   716→// cleanupDashboardForSave applies the same cleanup logic as the frontend\n   717→func cleanupDashboardForSave(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n   718→\tremoveNonPersistedProperties(dashboard)\n   719→\tremoveNullValues(dashboard)\n   720→\tcleanupTemplating(dashboard)\n   721→\tcleanupPanels(dashboard)\n   722→\tcleanupDashboardDefaults(dashboard)\n   723→}\n   724→\n   725→// removeNonPersistedProperties removes non-persisted dashboard properties\n   726→func removeNonPersistedProperties(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n   727→\tnonPersistedProperties := map[string]bool{\n   728→\t\t\"events\":                           true,\n   729→\t\t\"meta\":                             true,\n   730→\t\t\"panels\":                           true, // handled specially below\n   731→\t\t\"templating\":                       true, // handled specially below\n   732→\t\t\"originalTime\":                     true,\n   733→\t\t\"originalTemplating\":               true,\n   734→\t\t\"originalLibraryPanels\":            true,\n   735→\t\t\"panelInEdit\":                      true,\n   736→\t\t\"panelInView\":                      true,\n   737→\t\t\"getVariablesFromState\":            true,\n   738→\t\t\"formatDate\":                       true,\n   739→\t\t\"appEventsSubscription\":            true,\n   740→\t\t\"panelsAffectedByVariableChange\":   true,\n   741→\t\t\"lastRefresh\":                      true,\n   742→\t\t\"timeRangeUpdatedDuringEditOrView\": true,\n   743→\t\t\"originalDashboard\":                true,\n   744→\t}\n   745→\n   746→\tfor k, v := range nonPersistedProperties {\n   747→\t\t// Do not remove \"panels\" and \"templating\" here, as they are handled specially\n   748→\t\tif (k == \"panels\" || k == \"templating\") && v {\n   749→\t\t\tcontinue\n   750→\t\t}\n   751→\t\tif v {\n   752→\t\t\tdelete(dashboard, k)\n   753→\t\t}\n   754→\t}\n   755→\n   756→\t// Remove properties that frontend omits in getSaveModel\n   757→\tdelete(dashboard, \"variables\")\n   758→}\n   759→\n   760→// removeNullValues removes null values to match frontend's JSON.stringify/parse behavior\n   761→func removeNullValues(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n   762→\t// This handles gnetId: null and other null properties\n   763→\tremoveIfDefaultValue(dashboard, \"gnetId\", nil)\n   764→}\n   765→\n   766→// cleanupTemplating cleans up templating to match frontend's getTemplatingSaveModel behavior\n   767→func cleanupTemplating(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n   768→\tif templating, ok := dashboard[\"templating\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   769→\t\tremoveNullValuesRecursively(templating)\n   770→\t\tcleanupTemplatingVariables(templating)\n   771→\t}\n   772→}\n   773→\n   774→// cleanupTemplatingVariables applies variable adapter logic\n   775→func cleanupTemplatingVariables(templating map[string]interface{}) {\n   776→\tif list, ok := templating[\"list\"].([]interface{}); ok {\n   777→\t\tfor _, variableInterface := range list {\n   778→\t\t\tif variable, ok := variableInterface.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   779→\t\t\t\tcleanupVariable(variable)\n   780→\t\t\t}\n   781→\t\t}\n   782→\t}\n   783→}\n   784→\n   785→// map[string]interface{}{}\n\t}\n\tif panel[\"links\"] == nil {\n\t\tpanel[\"links\"] = []interface{}{}\n\t}\n\n\tif _, exists := panel[\"fieldConfig\"]; !exists {\n\t\tpanel[\"fieldConfig\"] = map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"defaults\":  map[string]interface{}{},\n\t\t\t\"overrides\": []interface{}{},\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\t// Add missing defaults and overrides (matches frontend defaultsDeep behavior)\n\t\tif fieldConfig, ok := panel[\"fieldConfig\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\tif _, hasDefaults := fieldConfig[\"defaults\"]; !hasDefaults {\n\t\t\t\tfieldConfig[\"defaults\"] = map[string]interface{}{}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif _, hasOverrides := fieldConfig[\"overrides\"]; !hasOverrides {\n\t\t\t\tfieldConfig[\"overrides\"] = []interface{}{}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif panel[\"title\"] == nil {\n\t\tpanel[\"title\"] = \"\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Auto-migration logic is now applied during cleanup phase to match frontend behavior\n\n\t// Structure normalizations\n\tensureQueryIds(panel)\n}\n\n// ensureTemplatingExists ensures templating.list exists\nfunc ensureTemplatingExists(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n\tif templating, ok := dashboard[\"templating\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\tif templating[\"list\"] == nil {\n\t\t\ttemplating[\"list\"] = []interface{}{}\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tdashboard[\"templating\"] = map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"list\": []interface{}{},\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// ensureAnnotationsExist ensures annotations.list exists\nfunc ensureAnnotationsExist(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n\tif annotations, ok := dashboard[\"annotations\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\tif annotations[\"list\"] == nil {\n\t\t\tannotations[\"list\"] = []interface{}{}\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tdashboard[\"annotations\"] = map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"list\": []interface{}{},\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// ensurePanelsHaveUniqueIds ensures all panels have unique IDs\nfunc ensurePanelsHaveUniqueIds(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n\tpanels := getPanels(dashboard)\n\tif len(panels) == 0 {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tids := make(map[float64]bool)\n\tnextPanelId := getNextPanelId(panels)\n\n\tfor _, panel := range panels {\n\t\tif panelID, ok := panel[\"id\"].(float64); ok && panelID > 0 {\n\t\t\tif ids[panelID] {\n\t\t\t\t// Duplicate ID found, assign new one\n\t\t\t\tpanel[\"id\"] = float64(nextPanelId)\n\t\t\t\tnextPanelId++\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Valid unique ID, keep it\n\t\t\t\tids[panelID] = true\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t// No ID or invalid ID, assign new one\n\t\t\tpanel[\"id\"] = float64(nextPanelId)\n\t\t\tnextPanelId++\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// getNextPanelId finds the next available panel ID\nfunc getNextPanelId(panels []map[string]interface{}) int {\n\tmax := 0\n\tfor _, panel := range panels {\n\t\tif panelID, ok := panel[\"id\"].(float64); ok && panelID > 0 {\n\t\t\tif int(panelID) > max {\n\t\t\t\tmax = int(panelID)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn max + 1\n}\n\n// sortPanelsByGridPos sorts panels by grid position (y first, then x)\nfunc sortPanelsByGridPos(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n\tpanels := getPanels(dashboard)\n\tif len(panels) == 0 {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tsort.SliceStable(panels, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\tpanelA := panels[i]\n\t\tpanelB := panels[j]\n\n\t\tgridPosA, okA := panelA[\"gridPos\"].(map[string]interface{})\n\t\tgridPosB, okB := panelB[\"gridPos\"].(map[string]interface{})\n\n\t\tif !okA || !okB {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tyA, okA := gridPosA[\"y\"].(float64)\n\t\tyB, okB := gridPosB[\"y\"].(float64)\n\n\t\tif !okA || !okB {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif yA == yB {\n\t\t\t// Same row, sort by x\n\t\t\txA, okA := gridPosA[\"x\"].(float64)\n\t\t\txB, okB := gridPosB[\"x\"].(float64)\n\n\t\t\tif !okA || !okB {\n\t\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\treturn xA < xB\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn yA < yB\n\t})\n}\n\n// addBuiltInAnnotationQuery adds the built-in \"Annotations & Alerts\" annotation\nfunc addBuiltInAnnotationQuery(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n\tannotations, ok := dashboard[\"annotations\"].(map[string]interface{})\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tlist, ok := annotations[\"list\"].([]interface{})\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Check if built-in annotation already exists\n\tfor _, item := range list {\n\t\tif annotation, ok := item.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\tif builtIn, ok := annotation[\"builtIn\"].(float64); ok && builtIn == 1 {\n\t\t\t\treturn // Already exists\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Add built-in annotation\n\tbuiltInAnnotation := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\"datasource\": map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"uid\":  \"-- Grafana --\",\n\t\t\t\"type\": \"grafana\",\n\t\t},\n\t\t\"name\":      \"Annotations & Alerts\",\n\t\t\"type\":      \"dashboard\",\n\t\t\"iconColor\": \"rgba(0, 211, 255, 1)\", // DEFAULT_ANNOTATION_COLOR\n\t\t\"enable\":    true,\n\t\t\"hide\":      true,\n\t\t\"builtIn\":   float64(1),\n\t}\n\n\t// Insert at the beginning\n\tannotations[\"list\"] = append([]interface{}{builtInAnnotation}, list...)\n}\n\n// initMeta initializes meta properties with defaults\nfunc initMeta(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n\tmeta, ok := dashboard[\"meta\"].(map[string]interface{})\n\tif !ok {\n\t\tmeta = make(map[string]interface{})\n\t\tdashboard[\"meta\"] = meta\n\t}\n\n\t// Apply defaults\n\tif meta[\"canShare\"] == nil {\n\t\tmeta[\"canShare\"] = true\n\t}\n\tif meta[\"canSave\"] == nil {\n\t\tmeta[\"canSave\"] = true\n\t}\n\tif meta[\"canStar\"] == nil {\n\t\tmeta[\"canStar\"] = true\n\t}\n\tif meta[\"canEdit\"] == nil {\n\t\tmeta[\"canEdit\"] = true\n\t}\n\tif meta[\"canDelete\"] == nil {\n\t\tmeta[\"canDelete\"] = true\n\t}\n\n\t// Derived properties\n\tmeta[\"showSettings\"] = meta[\"canEdit\"]\n\n\teditable, _ := dashboard[\"editable\"].(bool)\n\tif meta[\"canSave\"] == true && !editable {\n\t\tmeta[\"canMakeEditable\"] = true\n\t} else {\n\t\tmeta[\"canMakeEditable\"] = false\n\t}\n\n\tmeta[\"hasUnsavedFolderChange\"] = false\n\n\t// If dashboard is not editable, restrict permissions\n\tif !editable {\n\t\tmeta[\"canEdit\"] = false\n\t\tmeta[\"canDelete\"] = false\n\t\tmeta[\"canSave\"] = false\n\t}\n}\n\n// removeNullValuesFromVariables removes null values from variable.current.value\nfunc removeNullValuesFromVariables(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n\ttemplating, ok := dashboard[\"templating\"].(map[string]interface{})\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tlist, ok := templating[\"list\"].([]interface{})\n\tif !ok || len(list) == 0 {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, item := range list {\n\t\tif variable, ok := item.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\tif current, ok := variable[\"current\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\tif value, exists := current[\"value\"]; exists {\n\t\t\t\t\t// Check for null value\n\t\t\t\t\tif value == nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tdelete(current, \"value\")\n\t\t\t\t\t} else if valueArray, isArray := value.([]interface{}); isArray {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t// Check for null values in arrays\n\t\t\t\t\t\thasNull := false\n\t\t\t\t\t\tfor _, v := range valueArray {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif v == nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\thasNull = true\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t\tif hasNull {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdelete(current, \"value\")\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// ensureQueryIds ensures all queries have refId\nfunc ensureQueryIds(panel map[string]interface{}) {\n\ttargets, ok := panel[\"targets\"].([]interface{})\n\tif !ok || len(targets) == 0 {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Check if any target is missing refId\n\thasMissingRefId := false\n\tfor _, target := range targets {\n\t\tif targetMap, ok := target.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\tif targetMap[\"refId\"] == nil {\n\t\t\t\thasMissingRefId = true\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif hasMissingRefId {\n\t\t// Find existing refIds\n\t\texistingRefIds := make(map[string]bool)\n\t\tfor _, target := range targets {\n\t\t\tif targetMap, ok := target.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\tif refId, ok := targetMap[\"refId\"].(string); ok {\n\t\t\t\t\texistingRefIds[refId] = true\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Assign refIds to targets that don't have them\n\t\tletters := \"ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ\"\n\t\tletterIndex := 0\n\n\t\tfor _, target := range targets {\n\t\t\tif targetMap, ok := target.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\tif targetMap[\"refId\"] == nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t// Find next available refId\n\t\t\t\t\tfor letterIndex < len(letters) {\n\t\t\t\t\t\trefId := string(letters[letterIndex])\n\t\t\t\t\t\tif !existingRefIds[refId] {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\ttargetMap[\"refId\"] = refId\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\texistingRefIds[refId] = true\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t\tletterIndex++\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\tletterIndex++\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// getPanels extracts all panels from the dashboard (including nested panels)\n// This matches the frontend's depth-first iteration order in panelIterator()\nfunc getPanels(dashboard map[string]interface{}) []map[string]interface{} {\n\tvar panels []map[string]interface{}\n\n\t// Get top-level panels\n\tif dashboardPanels, ok := dashboard[\"panels\"].([]interface{}); ok {\n\t\tfor _, panelInterface := range dashboardPanels {\n\t\t\tif panel, ok := panelInterface.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\t// Add top-level panel first\n\t\t\t\tpanels = append(panels, panel)\n\n\t\t\t\t// Then add its nested panels (depth-first order)\n\t\t\t\tif nestedPanels, ok := panel[\"panels\"].([]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tfor _, nestedPanelInterface := range nestedPanels {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tif nestedPanel, ok := nestedPanelInterface.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tpanels = append(panels, nestedPanel)\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn panels\n}\n\n// cleanupPanelForSaveWithContext mimics the PanelModel.getSaveModel() behavior\n// This removes properties that shouldn't be persisted and filters out default values\nfunc cleanupPanelForSaveWithContext(panel map[string]interface{}, isNested bool) {\n\t// Apply auto-migration logic (matches frontend PanelModel constructor)\n\t// This happens during cleanup phase to match when frontend applies auto-migration\n\t// Only apply auto-migration to top-level panels, not nested ones (matches frontend behavior)\n\tif !isNested {\n\t\tapplyPanelAutoMigration(panel)\n\t}\n\n\t// Library panel specific cleanup (matches frontend behavior)\n\t// Frontend only preserves id, title, gridPos, and libraryPanel for library panels\n\tif libraryPanel, hasLibraryPanel := panel[\"libraryPanel\"]; hasLibraryPanel && libraryPanel != nil {\n\t\t// Create a new panel with only the essential properties\n\t\tessentialProps := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"id\":           panel[\"id\"],\n\t\t\t\"title\":        panel[\"title\"],\n\t\t\t\"gridPos\":      panel[\"gridPos\"],\n\t\t\t\"libraryPanel\": libraryPanel,\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Clear the original panel and copy back only essential properties\n\t\tfor key := range panel {\n\t\t\tdelete(panel, key)\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor key, value := range essentialProps {\n\t\t\tif value != nil {\n\t\t\t\tpanel[key] = value\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn // Skip the rest of the cleanup for library panels\n\t}\n\n\t// Row panel specific cleanup (matches frontend behavior)\n\tcleanupRowPanelProperties(panel)\n\n\t// Track which properties were present in the input to preserve them even if they become empty\n\toriginalProperties := make(map[string]bool)\n\tfor key := range panel {\n\t\toriginalProperties[key] = true\n\t}\n\t// Properties that should never be persisted (notPersistedProperties)\n\tnotPersistedProps := map[string]bool{\n\t\t\"events\":                  true,\n\t\t\"isViewing\":               true,\n\t\t\"isEditing\":               true,\n\t\t\"isInView\":                true,\n\t\t\"hasRefreshed\":            true,\n\t\t\"cachedPluginOptions\":     true, // This is the key one causing issues\n\t\t\"plugin\":                  true,\n\t\t\"queryRunner\":             true,\n\t\t\"replaceVariables\":        true,\n\t\t\"configRev\":               true,\n\t\t\"hasSavedPanelEditChange\": true,\n\t\t\"getDisplayTitle\":         true,\n\t\t\"dataSupport\":             true,\n\t\t\"key\":                     true,\n\t\t\"isNew\":                   true,\n\t\t\"refreshWhenInView\":       true,\n\t\t\"scopedVars\":              true, // Frontend removes scopedVars from save model\n\t}\n\n\t// Default values that should be filtered out if they match (defaults)\n\tdefaults := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\"gridPos\": map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"x\": float64(0), \"y\": float64(0), \"h\": float64(3), \"w\": float64(6),\n\t\t},\n\t\t\"targets\": []interface{}{\n\t\t\tmap[string]interface{}{\"refId\": \"A\"},\n\t\t},\n\t\t\"cachedPluginOptions\": map[string]interface{}{},\n\t\t\"transparent\":         false,\n\t\t\"options\":             map[string]interface{}{},\n\t\t\"links\":               []interface{}{},\n\t\t\"fieldConfig\": map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"defaults\":  map[string]interface{}{},\n\t\t\t\"overrides\": []interface{}{},\n\t\t},\n\t\t\"title\": \"\",\n\t}\n\n\t// Remove notPersistedProperties\n\tfor prop := range notPersistedProps {\n\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n\t}\n\n\t// Filter out properties that match defaults\n\tfor prop, defaultValue := range defaults {\n\t\tif panelValue, exists := panel[prop]; exists {\n\t\t\tif isEqual(panelValue, defaultValue) {\n\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Remove empty transformations array unless nested panel had them originally\n\tif transformations, ok := panel[\"transformations\"].([]interface{}); ok && len(transformations) == 0 {\n\t\tif panel[\"_originallyHadTransformations\"] != true || !isNested {\n\t\t\tdelete(panel, \"transformations\")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Remove null values recursively to match frontend's JSON.stringify/parse behavior\n\t// Pass panel type information to help with threshold handling\n\tpanelType := \"\"\n\tif t, ok := panel[\"type\"].(string); ok {\n\t\tpanelType = t\n\t}\n\tremoveNullValuesRecursivelyWithContext(panel, panelType)\n\n\t// Filter out properties that match defaults (matches frontend's isEqual logic)\n\tfilterDefaultValues(panel, originalProperties)\n\n\t// Clean up internal markers\n\tdelete(panel, \"_originallyHadTransformations\")\n\tdelete(panel, \"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\")\n}\n\n// filterDefaultValues removes properties that match the default values (matches frontend's isEqual logic)\nfunc filterDefaultValues(panel map[string]interface{}, originalProperties map[string]bool) {\n\t// Get panel type for panel-specific defaults\n\tpanelType := \"\"\n\tif t, ok := panel[\"type\"].(string); ok {\n\t\tpanelType = t\n\t}\n\n\t// PanelModel defaults from frontend\n\tdefaults := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\"gridPos\": map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"x\": 0, \"y\": 0, \"h\": 3, \"w\": 6,\n\t\t},\n\t\t\"targets\": []interface{}{\n\t\t\tmap[string]interface{}{\"refId\": \"A\"},\n\t\t},\n\t\t\"cachedPluginOptions\": map[string]interface{}{},\n\t\t\"transparent\":         false,\n\t\t\"options\":             map[string]interface{}{},\n\t\t\"links\":               []interface{}{},\n\t\t\"fieldConfig\": map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"defaults\":  map[string]interface{}{},\n\t\t\t\"overrides\": []interface{}{},\n\t\t},\n\t\t\"title\": \"\",\n\t}\n\n\t// Add panel-specific defaults\n\tif panelType == \"table\" {\n\t\t// Remove legacy table properties (matches frontend getSaveModel filtering)\n\t\t// Exception: preserve original properties for old table panels with autoMigrateFrom=\"table-old\"\n\t\tlegacyTableProps := []string{\"pageSize\", \"scroll\", \"fontSize\", \"showHeader\", \"sort\"}\n\t\tfor _, prop := range legacyTableProps {\n\t\t\tif _, exists := panel[prop]; exists {\n\t\t\t\tif autoMigrateFrom, hasAutoMigrate := panel[\"autoMigrateFrom\"]; hasAutoMigrate && autoMigrateFrom == \"table-old\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tif !originalProperties[prop] {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Remove properties that match defaults, but preserve properties that were originally present\n\tfor prop, defaultValue := range defaults {\n\t\tif panelValue, exists := panel[prop]; exists {\n\t\t\tif isEqual(panelValue, defaultValue) {\n\t\t\t\t// Special case: fieldConfig - handle preservation of original custom object first\n\t\t\t\tif prop == \"fieldConfig\" {\n\t\t\t\t\t// Check if we need to preserve the custom object before removing fieldConfig\n\t\t\t\t\tif panel[\"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\"] == true {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t// Ensure fieldConfig structure exists with custom object\n\t\t\t\t\t\tif fieldConfig, ok := panelValue.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif defaults, ok := fieldConfig[\"defaults\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif _, hasCustom := defaults[\"custom\"]; !hasCustom {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdefaults[\"custom\"] = map[string]interface{}{}\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t// Don't remove fieldConfig if we added custom back\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\t// Only remove if it wasn't originally present in the input\n\t\t\t\t\tif !originalProperties[prop] {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Remove empty targets arrays (frontend removes them in cleanup)\n\tremoveIfDefaultValue(panel, \"targets\", []interface{}{})\n\n\t// Handle case where fieldConfig was removed but originally had custom object\n\tif panel[\"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\"] == true {\n\t\tif _, hasFieldConfig := panel[\"fieldConfig\"]; !hasFieldConfig {\n\t\t\t// Recreate fieldConfig with custom object\n\t\t\tpanel[\"fieldConfig\"] = map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\"defaults\": map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\t\"custom\": map[string]interface{}{},\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t\"overrides\": []interface{}{},\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Clean up fieldConfig to match frontend behavior\n\tif fieldConfig, exists := panel[\"fieldConfig\"].(map[string]interface{}); exists {\n\t\t// Clean up fieldConfig defaults to match frontend behavior\n\t\tif defaults, hasDefaults := fieldConfig[\"defaults\"].(map[string]interface{}); hasDefaults {\n\t\t\t// Remove properties that frontend considers as defaults and omits\n\t\t\tcleanupFieldConfigDefaults(defaults, panel)\n\n\t\t\t// Preserve custom object if it was originally present, even if empty\n\t\t\tif panel[\"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\"] == true {\n\t\t\t\tif _, hasCustom := defaults[\"custom\"]; !hasCustom {\n\t\t\t\t\tdefaults[\"custom\"] = map[string]interface{}{}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// isEqual checks if two values are equal (simplified version)\nfunc isEqual(a, b interface{}) bool {\n\tif a == nil && b == nil {\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\tif a == nil || b == nil {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\t// For simple types, use direct comparison\n\tswitch aVal := a.(type) {\n\tcase bool:\n\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(bool); ok {\n\t\t\treturn aVal == bVal\n\t\t}\n\tcase string:\n\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(string); ok {\n\t\t\treturn aVal == bVal\n\t\t}\n\tcase float64:\n\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(float64); ok {\n\t\t\treturn aVal == bVal\n\t\t}\n\tcase []interface{}:\n\t\tif bVal, ok := b.([]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\tif len(aVal) != len(bVal) {\n\t\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfor i, v := range aVal {\n\t\t\t\tif !isEqual(v, bVal[i]) {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\tcase map[string]interface{}:\n\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\tif len(aVal) != len(bVal) {\n\t\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfor k, v := range aVal {\n\t\t\t\tif !isEqual(v, bVal[k]) {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn false\n}\n\n// cleanupDashboardForSave applies the same cleanup logic as the frontend\nfunc cleanupDashboardForSave(dashboard map[string]interface{}) If it's undefined, it skips the migration.\nBut it still processes overrides at line 659-669 regardless of whether `displayMode` was found in defaults.\n\nNow let me compare this to the Go backend code in v38.go:```go\ncustom, ok := defaults[\"custom\"].(map[string]interface{})\nif !ok {\n    continue\n}\n\n// Migrate displayMode to cellOptions\nif displayMode, exists := custom[\"displayMode\"]; exists {\n    if displayModeStr, ok := displayMode.(string); ok {\n        custom[\"cellOptions\"] = migrateTableDisplayModeToCellOptions(displayModeStr)\n    }\n    // Delete the legacy field\n    delete(custom, \"displayMode\")\n}\n\n// Update any overrides referencing the cell display mode\nmigrateOverrides(fieldConfig)\n```\n\nThe Go code checks if `custom` exists (line 120-123). If it doesn't, it continues (skips the entire panel). This means the `migrateOverrides` call at line 135 is never reached if `custom` doesn't exist.\n\nThe frontend is more lenient - it still processes overrides even if `displayMode` is not found in defaults.\n\nSo the bug is:\n1. A table panel from v10.3 (schema v37) doesn't have `fieldConfig.defaults.custom` explicitly set\n\n\n2. The backend v38 migration sees that `custom` doesn't exist and skips the entire panel\n3. The overrides with `custom.displayMode` properties never get migrated to `custom.cellOptions`\n4. When the frontend loads this, it finds `custom.displayMode` in the overrides but doesn't know what to do with it\n5. The field overrides are effectively ignored\n\nThe root cause is that the backend skips panels without `defaults.custom`, so override migrations never happen. The frontend still tries to handle overrides, creating a mismatch. I need to verify the schema versions to confirm this affects v10.3 to v10.4 This prevents the `migrateOverrides()` function from being called, which means field override properties that reference `custom.displayMode` never get migrated to `custom.cellOptions`.\n\n**Why It Fails:**\n- Dashboards saved in v10.3 without explicit `fieldConfig.defaults.custom` are not processed\n- Field override configurations that apply column-level formatting are left unmigrated\n- When v10.4 renders these tables, it looks for `custom.cellOptions` but finds the old `custom.displayMode` format, which it ignores\n\n**Why Some Dashboards Work:**\n- Dashboards with explicit `fieldConfig.defaults.custom` in their JSON pass the type assertion and are processed correctly\n- All test fixtures only cover this working case, missing the regression scenario\n\n**Evidence:**\n- Backend: `v38.go` skips processing if `custom` doesn't exist (line 120-123)\n- Frontend: `DashboardMigrator.ts` (lines 644-674) handles this more gracefully by still processing overrides even when defaults lack displayMode\n\nThe full detailed report with all files, functions, and recommendations has been written to `/logs/agent/investigation.md`."}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":7,"cache_creation_input_tokens":932,"cache_read_input_tokens":68189,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":932},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"cb296321-15c5-4144-84e7-885fac7b7719","uuid":"e05e6821-f483-4758-bb40-cd553601b025"}
